### Chapter 14: Ch 12: Marriage—Free Love
### 5:43:465 hours, 43 minutes, 46 seconds12 marriage free love think not that I am come to destroy
### 5:43:535 hours, 43 minutes, 53 secondsthe law or the prophets I am not come to destroy but to fulfill Jesus sermon man as a finite and
### 5:44:035 hours, 44 minutes, 3 secondsrelational being is the subject of government being produced in developed by laws acting to certain ends he is the

### 5:44:185 hours, 44 minutes, 18 secondstheir action upon his conscious perceptions and affections man as a conscious being is the subject of two
### 5:44:255 hours, 44 minutes, 25 secondsclasses of impulses one is a sense of affinity the other of restraint the first is the natural impulse proceeding
### 5:44:345 hours, 44 minutes, 34 secondsfrom certain relations and is a spontaneous proceeding from such relation without considering consequences the other is a reflex
### 5:44:425 hours, 44 minutes, 42 secondsimpulse proceeding from supposed consequences which will follow certain conditions and actions and has respect
### 5:44:495 hours, 44 minutes, 49 secondsto ends or uses this latter class of impulses makes him the subject of outward motions and bring him under the
### 5:44:585 hours, 44 minutes, 58 secondsDominion of laws external to his being as such he becomes the subject of an external government as a conscious being
### 5:45:075 hours, 45 minutes, 7 secondsman is the subject of two classes of external government the one which appeals to his selfish and lustful nature and the other which appeals to
### 5:45:155 hours, 45 minutes, 15 secondshis moral and relational nature and he is the proper subject of the one or the other government according to the character of his ruling affection or
### 5:45:245 hours, 45 minutes, 24 secondslove man as a conscious being can be governed only through some Department of his Consciousness that which induces in him
